### EMAIL: [ACTION REQUIRED] Cloudinary Deprecation
ID: 19b93f3e91c34d71
From: Elio Esteves Duarte <elio.duarte@hellofresh.com>
----------------------------------------

Hi everyone,



We've migrated our media asset hosting from Cloudinary to ImageKit. We have

already migrated our images on the websites and apps. However, we are still

receiving requests on Cloudinary from sites like operations.hellofresh.com

and blog.hellofresh.com.



*What You Need to Do*



Check if you're using images hosted directly on Cloudinary (domain:

*res.cloudinary.com

<http://res.cloudinary.com>*). If so, you have two options:



*Option 1: Update the Cloudinary URL*



In most cases, the image already exists in our S3 bucket. Replace the

Cloudinary URL with the new format:



*Before (Cloudinary):*

*https://res.cloudinary.com/hellofresh/image/upload/f_auto,fl_lossy,q_auto/v1/hellofresh_s3/image/5c005823c445fa20282d0752-d318f9dd.jpg

<https://res.cloudinary.com/hellofresh/image/upload/f_auto,fl_lossy,q_auto/v1/hellofresh_s3/image/5c005823c445fa20282d0752-d318f9dd.jpg>*



*After (ImageKit):*

*https://media.hellofresh.com/hellofresh_s3/image/5c005823c445fa20282d0752-d318f9dd.jpg

<https://media.hellofresh.com/hellofresh_s3/image/5c005823c445fa20282d0752-d318f9dd.jpg>*



*Option 2: Upload the Image to S3*

If the URL rewrite didn't work, upload the image to our S3 bucket.



   1. Access our S3 bucket: hf-website-live

   <https://eu-west-1.console.aws.amazon.com/s3/buckets/hf-website-live?region=eu-west-1>

   .





   1. Change the URL to the following format:

*https://media.hellofresh.com/hellofresh_website/path/to/image/in/bucket.jpg

   <https://med

<@U027201FQSV> <@U01AKGWGLC8> <@U08E2S3V5D1>, I wanted to flag an issue when using recurring meal selections through KRS in case you're not aware of it already. The issue occurs whenever the user:
‚Ä¢ Does a meal selection which triggers KRS
‚Ä¢ Changes their plan to something else without going through another meal selection
‚Ä¢ All the user's future deliveries remain on the old SKU eventhough their plan was successfully updated
You can find more details about <https://hellofresh.slack.com/archives/C06CE7FB951/p1765808926304309|this issue here>, I've already confirmed with <@U01AKGWGLC8>that this also affects GoC. In TPT we implemented a short term solution of triggering a meal selection after change plan.

### SLACK: diy-research - 2026-01-06 18:19:25
User: Amie Mackay
----------------------------------------

NEW DIY results, submitted and analyzed by <@U02G0RL6UCW>, <@U094H4HAJSJ>, &amp; <@U01G62WHYKB>.
:hellofreshhhh: *<https://hellofresh.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/UR/pages/5830901796/DIY+Loyalty+2.0|DIY: Loyalty 2.0 (HF)>* :hellofreshhhh:

:mag: *Overview:* This concept test evaluated a proposed redesign of the HelloFresh Loyalty Program, with a focus on user expectations, dashboard usability, and redemption flow clarity. We aimed to understand where users expect to find loyalty features, how they interpret the mechanics of points and rewards, and what frictions exist in the current redemption experience.
:link:*See: <https://www.figma.com/proto/2t9LKngEQoPGkiuqiiBaqH/prototype?page-id=0%3A1&amp;node-id=1-8571&amp;p=f&amp;viewport=427%2C191%2C0.14&amp;t=AuyQRDcN2QoOqcZK-1&amp;scaling=scale-down&amp;content-scaling=fixed&amp;starting-point-node-id=1%3A8571&amp;hotspot-hints=0|prototype design>*

:chart_with_upwards_trend: *Results:* Most users correctly identified the Loyalty Program as a tiered, points-based system and expected to find it within their Profile section‚Äîviewed as a natural hub for account and reward information. While users appreciated the core elements (e.g., tiers, points, and reward logic), confusion arose around generic ‚ÄúDiscounts,‚Äù which felt inconsistent with earned rewards. The biggest usability issues stemmed from abrupt transitions, auto-applied redemptions, and lack of clarity around earning mechanics. Users voiced a strong desire for a visible point balance, clearer reward application, and a manual toggle at checkout. These insights will inform design refinements focused on transparency, navigation, and control.
CC: <@U0341220M0E>

*Executive Summary:*
On 2026-01-05, VMS business showed strong top-of-funnel performance with 1,079 landing page views (+370 vs. prior week) and maintained solid order completion at 15 successful orders (+4 vs. prior week). However, conversion efficiency declined with signup page views dropping to 28 (-17 vs. prior week), indicating potential friction in the mid-funnel despite strong traffic acquisition. *Key Insights:*
‚Ä¢ Strong traffic growth with landing page views reaching 1,079 (+18% day-over-day, +52% week-over-week), suggesting effective marketing or seasonal demand
‚Ä¢ Successful orders remained stable at 15 units (flat day-over-day, +36% week-over-week), maintaining the business momentum from recent weeks
‚Ä¢ Conversion funnel shows concerning mid-stage weakness: signup page views dropped 15 day-over-day and 17 week-over-week, creating a bottleneck between product interest and purchase intent
‚Ä¢ Products page engagement remained strong at 2,049 views with healthy checkout conversion (84 checkout views), but the signup step appears to be the primary conversion barrier
‚Ä¢ Weekly trend analysis shows consistent order growth (4-15 range) with 2026-01-05 matching the previous day's peak performance, indicating sustainable business momentum

### SLACK: consumer-mega-alliance - 2026-01-06 20:00:05
User: Lucas Freire Torres Cruz
----------------------------------------

:mega: *[Deprecation Announcement] Legacy Whitelabel Mobile App & Repository* :mega:

*TL;DR*
‚Ä¢ With all HelloFresh Group mobile apps now being powered by the Unified Mobile App Infra, the legacy *whitelabel-mobile* app and repository are being fully deprecated
‚Ä¢ *Jan 6, 2026:* Force update to Unified App (Android 25.51 | iOS 25.51.1)
‚Ä¢ *Jan 31, 2026:* Full shutdown of CI/CD, services, and repository archiving
‚Ä¢ Only legacy-specific infrastructure is affected ‚Äî Unified App services continue as usual
________________________________________________________________________

Hi HelloFresh Team,

We're pleased to announce the *deprecation of the legacy whitelabel-mobile app* and repository which proudly supported brands such as EveryPlate :everyplate:, ChefsPlate :chefs_plate2:, GreenChef :greenchef:, Factor :factor:, Youfoodz :youfoodz-logo-light-green: and HelloFresh Japan :hfau::jp:.

As part of our continued consolidation into the *Unified Mobile App (shared-mobile-modules) which will power all HelloFresh Group mobile apps moving forward*, all legacy infrastructure, CI/CD pipelines, and brand-specific configurations for the whitelabel-mobile repository will be permanently shut down.
________________________________________________________________________

:calendar: *Key Dates*

*Tuesday, January 6th, 2026 (Week 03) - Force Update*
‚Ä¢ Legacy app users blocked and prompted to update to Unified App
‚Ä¢ Minimum versions enforced: 25.50
*By Friday, January 31st, 2026 - Full Shutdown*
‚Ä¢ All CI/CD pipelines disabled
‚Ä¢ Unique Third-party services shut down
‚Ä¢ Repository archived
________________________________________________________________________

:red_circle: *Services Being Shut Down*

*CI/CD*
‚Ä¢ Bitrise workflows, 
‚Ä¢ GitHub Actions, 
‚Ä¢ /bitrise Slack bot
*Analytics*
‚Ä¢ Statsig legacy flags
‚Ä¢ Adjust legacy events
‚Ä¢ GTM legacy container
‚Ä¢ Firebase legacy streams
‚Ä¢ Error TrackingSentry project whitelabel-mobile
‚Ä¢ BigQuery monitoring
*Monitoring*
‚Ä¢ Sentry legacy streams
‚Ä¢ SonarQube project, 
‚Ä¢ FAB4 metrics, 
‚Ä¢ Slack Channels <#C01CL7Q6VJR|> <#C03T3PWL8KY|> <#GJMNKUJG2|> <#C019X60H9CY|> <#C051BFC6DQ8|>
*Content* 
‚Ä¢ Contentful legacy models
‚Ä¢ RCS configs
:alert:  *`IMPORTANT`:* Most third-party services (Firebase, Salesforce, Adjust, etc.) will continue operating for the Unified Mobile App. *We're only shutting down legacy-specific configurations and CI/CD infrastructure for the whitelabel-mobile repository*.
________________________________________________________________________

:one-team: *Impact*

*Customers*
All customers across our 6 live mobile apps (EveryPlate, ChefsPlate, GreenChef, Factor, Youfoodz, HelloFresh) have been successfully migrated to the new Unified Mobile App. *There is no impact to customers.*

*Internal Teams*
*Engineering:* Mobile, Platform, QA, RTE
*Support:* CS, On-call
*Product/Business:* PMs, Marketing, Analytics

We have been working with relevant teams throughout 2025 to ensure smooth onboarding and up-to-date integrations are enabled in the new app infrastructure. All affected services have replacement configurations in the Unified Mobile App to ensure business continuity after deprecation.
________________________________________________________________________

:question:*Questions or Support*

Please reach out in Slack: <#C019X60H9CY|>
________________________________________________________________________

Thank you for your cooperation during this transition. The Unified Mobile App simplifies our architecture and improves development velocity. :blob-thanks:
